					<h3>Speech</h3>
	
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="SPE100" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 100 &nbsp; Pronunciation and Communication for Non-Native Speakers (4)</h4>
				
													<p><strong>Corequisites:</strong> ESL 100, ESL 104 and suggested Co-requisite ESL 107</p>
								
				<p>For the non-native speaker of English, this course focuses on pronunciation improvement. By learning the American style of intonation, rhythm, speech production,and syllable stress, speech will be more understandable, articulate and expressive. Small group and individual communication activities, both speaking and listening, will reinforce these skills. This course is open to non-native speakers of English who are at an intermediate level or above.&nbsp; Students must take the Compass ESL test.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em;  background: #f0f0f0 ">
				<h4 id="SPE101" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 101 &nbsp; Oral Communication (3)</h4>
				
												
				<p>Focus on importance of communication competence in a variety of situations. Topics include verbal and nonverbal communication, listening, perception, self-concept, small group communication, and public speaking. Students required to prepare and present three to four graded oral presentations.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																																										<img src="/images/icons/online2.png" alt="Online"  style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																																										<img src="/images/icons/hybrid2.png" alt="Hybrid"  style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
															</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="SPE102" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 102 &nbsp; Public Speaking (3)</h4>
				
												
				<p>In-depth look at art of public speaking. Expands knowledge of ideas and concepts presented in SPE 101. Focus on presenting additional types of speeches, including business and organizational, ceremonial, speeches of tribute, acceptance, and toasting.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																																																<img src="/images/icons/hybrid2.png" alt="Hybrid"  style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
															</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em;  background: #f0f0f0 ">
				<h4 id="SPE103" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 103 &nbsp; Persuasion (3)</h4>
				
												
				<p>Skills necessary to become informed and critical consumer of persuasive messages. Persuasion examined through popular culture, advertising, politics, and mass media. Insights given into language use and symbols, nonverbal communication, and cultural and psychological approaches to persuasion.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="SPE104" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 104 &nbsp; Small Group Communication (3)</h4>
				
												
				<p>Study of process of group communication. Focus on group development, group roles, decision-making, leadership, power, and conflict management. How to be more productive member of group by acquiring skills to enhance group interaction.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em;  background: #f0f0f0 ">
				<h4 id="SPE105" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 105 &nbsp; Interviewing (3)</h4>
				
												
				<p>Focuses on art of interviewing in variety of contexts. Topics include types and uses of questions, common question pitfalls, listening, verbal and nonverbal communication, and specialized types of interviews such as journalistic, survey, persuasive, employment, performance review, counseling, and health care.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="SPE110" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 110 &nbsp; Interpersonal Communication (3)</h4>
				
												
				<p>How to become more informed and skillful communicators in diverse social world and more aware of how and why misunderstandings arise in communication among people whose dissimilar backgrounds and identities lead them to have different views about what communication means and does. Topics include dealing with difficult people, expression of emotions, assertiveness training, and conflict management.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em;  background: #f0f0f0 ">
				<h4 id="SPE115" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 115 &nbsp; Voice and Diction (3)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> SPE 101</p>
												
				<p>Study of the development and understanding of respiration, phonation, resonation, articulation, and diction. Credit not available for both SPE 115 and THE 115.</p>

																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="SPE200" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 200 &nbsp; Argumentation and Debate (3)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> SPE 101</p>
												
				<p>The discovery, support, and critical evaluation of intelligent arguments and decisions. Studies argument, evidence, reasoning, and oral advocacy; includes investigation, research, and critical analysis of claims and establishment of truth through proof.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em;  background: #f0f0f0 ">
				<h4 id="SPE201" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 201 &nbsp; Leadership Theory and Development (3)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> Take one- SPE 101, SPE 102, SPE 110 or instructor consent</p>
												
				<p>Leadership, the ability to influence other's behaviors and thoughts to accomplish a goal, is a responsibility faced in a variety of personal and professional contexts. Learn what it means to be a leader, how different leadership styles are utilized and how cultural, ethical and moral pressures affect leadership. Students will identify areas for personal growth and improvement in leadership positions as they learn and develop their own leadership skills, values, ethics and morals. Examination of leadership theory and development will be from a variety of backgrounds.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="SPE205" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">SPE 205 &nbsp; Gender Communication (3)</h4>
				
												
				<p>Answers to questions that confound women's and men's attempts to communicate with each other. Topics include gender construction through one's culture, portrayal of men and women in media, male and female approaches to conversation, role of power and empowerment in marriage and families, gender relations in workplace, and men and women in education.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">

																											</p>
			</div>

									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> SPE 101</p>

				<p>Explores issues related to intercultural communication process. Considers important role of context (social, cultural, and historical) in intercultural interactions. Topics include stereotyping, prejudice, ethnocentrism, social class and religious identities, folk culture, power, and intercultural conflict.</p>

									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> SPE 101</p>
												
				<p>Role of and development of professional communication skills intrinsic to the workplace.&nbsp; Focus is on the development of theoretical and performance competencies in interpersonal communication, small group communication, organizational communication and public communication.&nbsp; Includes understanding organizational diversity and ethics; improving listening skills; enhancing interviewing skills; managing group meetings and teamwork; and presentation of informational and persuasive proposals via enhancement of verbal, vocal and visual strategies.</p>

					<h3>Welding</h3>
	
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="WLD101" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 101 &nbsp; Introduction to Welding (3)</h4>
				
													<p><strong>Corequisites:</strong> WLD 111</p>
								
				<p>This covers basic work, health and safety information involved in the profession of welding, including the interpretation of welding symbols and sketches or drawings, and fabricating parts from sketches or drawings.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em;  background: #f0f0f0 ">
				<h4 id="WLD111" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 111 &nbsp; Thermal Cutting (2)</h4>
				
													<p><strong>Corequisites:</strong> WLD 101</p>
								
				<p>In this course students will learn to set up and perform straight square edge, shape square edge and straight bevel edge manual oxyfuel gas cuts (OFC) and plasma arc cuts (PAC) on various metals, perform OFC scarfing and gouging operations on carbon steel, and inspect and repair equipment used in cutting operations.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="WLD121" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 121 &nbsp; Shielded Metal Arc Welding I (4)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> WLD 101; WLD 111</p>
												
				<p>In this course students will learn the basic skills and knowledge needed to set up Shielded Metal Arc Welding (SMAW) equipment, choose appropriate electrodes, and perform SMAW operations on carbon steel.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em;  background: #f0f0f0 ">
				<h4 id="WLD122" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 122 &nbsp; Shielded Metal Arc Welding II (4)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> WLD 121</p>
												
				<p> This course expands on the techniques learned in WLD 121. Advanced welding techniques in Shielded Metal Arc Welding (SMAW) required of AWS Advanced level welders will be covered.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="WLD125" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 125 &nbsp; Welding Inspection and Testing (2)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> WLD 101; WLD 111; WLD 121</p>
												
				<p>This welding class covers weld inspections and weld testing practices for the new welder; including how to examine cut surfaces and edges of prepared base metal parts; how to examine tack, root passes, intermediate layers, and completed welds.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em;  background: #f0f0f0 ">
				<h4 id="WLD131" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 131 &nbsp; Gas Metal Arc Welding I (4)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> WLD 101; WLD 111</p>
												
				<p>In this course students will learn the basic skills and knowledge needed to set up Gas Metal Arc Welding (GMAW) equipment, choose appropriate electrodes, and perform GMAW-S and GMAW (spray) operations on carbon steel.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="WLD132" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 132 &nbsp; Gas Metal Arc Welding II (4)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> WLD 131</p>
												
				<p>This course expands on the techniques learned in WLD 131. Advanced welding techniques in Gas Metal Arc Welding (GMAW) required of AWS Advanced level welders will be covered.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em;  background: #f0f0f0 ">
				<h4 id="WLD141" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 141 &nbsp; Flux Cored Arc Welding I (4)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> WLD 101; WLD 111</p>
												
				<p>In this course students will learn the basic skills and knowledge needed to set up Flux Cored Arc Welding (FCAW) equipment, choose appropriate electrodes, and perform FCAW-G/GM and FCAW-S operations on carbon fuel.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="WLD142" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 142 &nbsp; Flux Cored Arc Welding II (4)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> WLD 141</p>
												
				<p>This course expands on the techniques learned in WLD 141. Advanced welding techniques in Flux Cored Arc Welding (FCAW) required of AWS Advanced level welders will be covered.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em;  background: #f0f0f0 ">
				<h4 id="WLD151" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 151 &nbsp; Gas Tungsten Arc Welding I (4)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> WLD 101; WLD 111</p>
												
				<p>In this course students will learn the basic skills and knowledge needed to set up Gas Tungsten Arc Welding (GTAW) equipment, choose appropriate electrodes and perform GTAW operations on carbon steel, austenitic stainless steel, and aluminum.</p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
					<div style="padding: 0 1em; ">
				<h4 id="WLD152" style="margin-top: 0; padding-top: 1em;">WLD 152 &nbsp; Gas Tungsten Arc Welding II (4)</h4>
				
									<p><strong>Prerequisites:</strong> WLD 151</p>
												
				<p>This course expands on the techniques learned in WLD 151. Advanced welding techniques in Gas Tungsten Arc Welding (GTAW) required of AWS Advanced level welders will be covered.<p>
				
				<p style="margin-top: -10px;">
					<span style="margin-right: .5rem; vertical-align: super;">Course Type(s):</span>
																		<img src="/images/icons/on-campus2.png" alt="On-Campus" style="margin-right: .75rem; vertical-align: middle;" />
																											</p>
			</div>
			
        <div id="sidebarLanding" class="showMobile"></div> 
   				</div><!-- #rightColumn-->
